<p><b>Marcus Rashford</b> <span class="noexcerpt nowraplinks" style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Order of the British Empire">MBE</a></span> (born 31 October 1997) is an English professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and the <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England national team</a>.
</p><p>A Manchester United player from the age of seven, Rashford scored two goals on both his first-team debut against <a href="/wiki/FC_Midtjylland" title="FC Midtjylland">Midtjylland</a> in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> in February 2016 and his Premier League debut against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> three days later. He also scored in his first <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester derby</a>, as well as on his <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debuts. With United, Rashford has so far won the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a>, EFL Cup, <a href="/wiki/FA_Community_Shield" title="FA Community Shield">FA Community Shield</a> and Europa League.
</p><p>Rashford scored on his England debut in May 2016, becoming the youngest English player to score in his first senior international match. He played at the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a> as the tournament's youngest player, and also represented England at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.
</p><p>Rashford also publicly campaigns on the issues of <a href="/wiki/Homelessness_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Homelessness in the United Kingdom">homelessness</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hunger_in_the_United_Kingdom#Among_children" title="Hunger in the United Kingdom">child hunger</a> in the United Kingdom, and has been praised for using his platform to be a political activist and philanthropist to drive societal change. For his efforts, he has received widespread praise and acclaim, and has been recognised for his efforts from institutions and organisations both in and out of sport.
</p>

<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-15"><a href="#Style_of_play,_development_and_comparisons"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Style of play, development and comparisons</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-16"><a href="#Charity_and_activism"><span class="tocnumber">5</span> <span class="toctext">Charity and activism</span></a>
<ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span></h2>
<p>Marcus Rashford<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> was born on 31 October 1997.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He was born in <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a>, Greater Manchester,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and was raised in the <a href="/wiki/Wythenshawe" title="Wythenshawe">Wythenshawe</a> area of the city.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He is of Kittitian descent, with his grandmother being born on the <a href="/wiki/West_Indies" title="West Indies">West Indies</a> island of <a href="/wiki/Saint_Kitts" title="Saint Kitts">Saint Kitts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Rashford comes from a <a href="/wiki/Working_class" title="Working class">working class</a> family; his mother is Melanie Maynard, a <a href="/wiki/Single_parent" title="Single parent">single parent</a> who often had to work multiple jobs to feed their family, sometimes skipping meals herself to ensure Rashford and his siblings ate.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-RashfordSuperhero_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashfordSuperhero-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He has four older siblings; two brothers, Dwaine Maynard and Dane Rashford, both of whom went on to represent him professionally,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and two sisters, Chantelle and Claire.<sup id="cite_ref-RashfordSuperhero_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashfordSuperhero-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He is a cousin of fellow footballer <a href="/wiki/Lois_Maynard" title="Lois Maynard">Lois Maynard</a>, who currently plays as a midfielder for <a href="/wiki/Stockport_County_F.C." title="Stockport County F.C.">Stockport County</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Rashford attended the <a href="/wiki/Ashton-on-Mersey_School" title="Ashton-on-Mersey School">Ashton-on-Mersey School</a>, a school where United have sent their academy players since 1998 and located close to their <a href="/wiki/Trafford_Training_Centre" title="Trafford Training Centre">Carrington</a> training ground;<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCMaking_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCMaking-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> he studied for a <a href="/wiki/Business_and_Technology_Education_Council#School_leaving_qualification_(Level_3)" title="Business and Technology Education Council">Business and Technology Education Council</a> (BTEC) National Diploma in Sport.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span></h3>
<p>Rashford began playing football for <a href="/w/index.php?title=Fletcher_Moss_Rangers_F.C.&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Fletcher Moss Rangers F.C. (page does not exist)">Fletcher Moss Rangers</a> at the age of five,<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> starting out as a goalkeeper, and cited former United goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Tim_Howard" title="Tim Howard">Tim Howard</a> as his goalkeeping idol.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNJourney_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNJourney-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Fletcher Ross Rangers academy development officer Dave Horrocks recalls that Rashford was on a "different level" to other boys, playing a major role as the team won a tournament with 15 scouts from various clubs watching.<sup id="cite_ref-FFTMWMH_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FFTMWMH-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He spent a week training with <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> before he joined the academy system at <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> at the age of seven, amid interest from <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FFTInt_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FFTInt-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He credited his brothers with helping him decide to join United.<sup id="cite_ref-Academy4000_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Academy4000-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Former United youth coach <a href="/wiki/Paul_McGuinness_(footballer)" title="Paul McGuinness (footballer)">Paul McGuinness</a> quickly saw Rashford's potential due to his athleticism both on and off the ball,<sup id="cite_ref-FFTMWMH_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FFTMWMH-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> but during his early years at the club, he often had to miss training as he found it difficult to get to training due to his mother and brothers working, and eventually received assistance from youth coaches Dave Bushell, Eamon Mulvey, and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Whelan" title="Tony Whelan">Tony Whelan</a>, who helped find drivers for Rashford to get to the training ground.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> When he was 11, he became the youngest ever player to be selected for the Manchester United Schoolboy Scholars scheme, usually reserved for players 12 and above.<sup id="cite_ref-FFTMWMH_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FFTMWMH-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He was fastracked and began playing cage football with <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jesse_Lingard" title="Jesse Lingard">Jesse Lingard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ravel_Morrison" title="Ravel Morrison">Ravel Morrison</a>, helping to increase his skill level playing with players four years his senior.<sup id="cite_ref-FFTMWMH_19-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FFTMWMH-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Rash12_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rash12-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2012, he was part of the Manchester United under-15 squad which finished second in the 23rd annual Marveld tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> named him as Manchester United's best prospect in the 2014 Next Generation, saying that his "<a href="/wiki/Total_Football" title="Total Football">total-football</a> style gives him a fair chance of going all the way".<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Rashford trained with United's first team for the first time aged 16 under the management of <a href="/wiki/David_Moyes" title="David Moyes">David Moyes</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2013–14 Manchester United F.C. season">2013–14 season</a>, and described the training session as "priceless" to himself and other <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" title="Manchester United F.C. Reserves and Academy">United academy players</a>; he began training with the first team more regularly, and was deemed a "high flier" by coaches.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNJourney_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNJourney-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2015, United Under-19s manager <a href="/wiki/Nicky_Butt" title="Nicky Butt">Nicky Butt</a> praised Rashford's performances for the team in a <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Youth_League_group_stage" title="2015–16 UEFA Youth League group stage">group stage</a> match of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Youth_League" title="UEFA Youth League">UEFA Youth League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> His inclusion in the team began following an injury to <a href="/wiki/Demetri_Mitchell" title="Demetri Mitchell">Demetri Mitchell</a>, and he capitalised on his chance by scoring six goals in 11 games in the Under-18's Premier League, as well as three goals in the Youth League.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He was awarded the captaincy of the team by Butt, who hailed him as a leader.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Rashford was named on the first-team bench for the first time on 21 November by <a href="/wiki/Louis_van_Gaal" title="Louis van Gaal">Louis van Gaal</a> for a <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>, which Manchester United won 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He received the number 39 squad number, due to Van Gaal's insistence that strikers wear a squad number containing a nine.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> The following week against <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>, he was again named on the bench, but was again unused in a 1–1 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In February 2016, Rashford was subject to a loan bid from <a href="/wiki/EFL_League_One" title="EFL League One">EFL League One</a> team <a href="/wiki/Crewe_Alexandra_F.C." title="Crewe Alexandra F.C.">Crewe Alexandra</a>, but the temporary transfer was rejected by Reserves manager <a href="/wiki/Warren_Joyce" title="Warren Joyce">Warren Joyce</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Former teammate <a href="/wiki/Sean_Goss" title="Sean Goss">Sean Goss</a> described how Rashford impressed in first-team training sessions while the club was suffering an injury crisis, despite being one of the younger players called up to train.<sup id="cite_ref-RashRise_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashRise-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season:_Debut"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season:_Debut">2015–16 season: Debut</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He's a very good young player. I see some of myself in him for sure – he has courage and he's fast and is very good with the ball. I think for the strikers they have to be hungry to score and I see that with him. He has an amazing future."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Rashford's idol <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> hailed him after his breakthrough in 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Marcus_Rashford.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Marcus_Rashford.jpg/170px-Marcus_Rashford.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="203" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Marcus_Rashford.jpg/255px-Marcus_Rashford.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Marcus_Rashford.jpg/340px-Marcus_Rashford.jpg 2x" data-file-width="742" data-file-height="888" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Marcus_Rashford.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rashford warming up for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in 2016</div></div></div>
<p>On 25 February 2016, Rashford was included in the 18-man squad for United's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> round of 32, second leg tie against Danish club <a href="/wiki/FC_Midtjylland" title="FC Midtjylland">Midtjylland</a>, owing to an injury crisis which saw 13 players injured.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Martial" title="Anthony Martial">Anthony Martial</a> was injured in the warm-up, Rashford was chosen to start the game, and marked his first-team debut with two goals in the second half of a 5–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Rashford's goals made him Manchester United's youngest ever scorer in European competition, beating a record previously held by <a href="/wiki/George_Best" title="George Best">George Best</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> and which was later broken by <a href="/wiki/Mason_Greenwood" title="Mason Greenwood">Mason Greenwood</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2019–20 Manchester United F.C. season">2019–20</a> season.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Rashford made his Premier League debut against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> three days later; he again scored twice and provided the assist for the other goal in a 3–2 home victory against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C.%E2%80%93Manchester_United_F.C._rivalry" title="Arsenal F.C.–Manchester United F.C. rivalry">their rivals</a>, making him the third youngest scorer for United in Premier League history after <a href="/wiki/Federico_Macheda" title="Federico Macheda">Federico Macheda</a> and <a href="/wiki/Danny_Welbeck" title="Danny Welbeck">Danny Welbeck</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Van Gaal hailed his performance as "fantastic" and better than his first match,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> but urged caution from the press not to harass and hype him, feeling he had the character to cope.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>On 20 March, Rashford made history when he scored the only goal in the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester derby</a>, his team's first away league win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> since 2012; aged just 18 years and 141 days, he became the youngest ever scorer in the fixture in the Premier League era, overtaking Wayne Rooney's record by almost one year.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> sixth-round replay against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a> on 13 April, Rashford scored a fantastic curled goal in a 2–1 win to help United advance to the semi-final.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored the only goal of the game against <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>, who were subsequently relegated for the first time since 1987.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He later led the line in the <a href="/wiki/2016_FA_Cup_Final" title="2016 FA Cup Final">FA Cup Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> on 21 May, which ended in a 2–1 victory marking United's 12th FA Cup win and Rashford's first piece of silverware.<sup id="cite_ref-2016FAC_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2016FAC-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He wrapped up the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2015–16 Manchester United F.C. season">season</a> with 8 goals in 18 appearances, despite only debuting in February, as well as winning the <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Murphy_Young_Player_of_the_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="Jimmy Murphy Young Player of the Year">Jimmy Murphy Young Player of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-YPOTY_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-YPOTY-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On 30 May, Rashford signed a new contract with United worth £20,000 a week, which would keep him at the club until 2020, with an option to extend for a further year.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season:_European_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season:_European_success">2016–17 season: European success</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"I see Rashford as a huge talent, I have been here two weeks and I also saw him last season. I get to see him live every day now and he is the future of England. He just needs to keep working hard, keep focusing and everything will come by itself."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Rashford's teammate <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> after joining the club in 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="189" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="594" data-file-height="661" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Marcus_Rashford_September_2016_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rashford lining up for United in 2016</div></div></div>
<p>For the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2016–17 Manchester United F.C. season">new season</a>, marking his place as part of the senior squad, Rashford was given the number 19 by new manager <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> The signing of veteran striker <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> meant he often had to settle for a place on the substitutes bench.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Rashford scored his first goal of the season on 27 August 2016 against <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a> in tremendous fashion, scoring in the second minute of injury time after coming on for <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mata" title="Juan Mata">Juan Mata</a> in the 71st minute.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He scored thrice more the next month, on 18 September in a 3–1 league defeat to Watford; on 21 September in a 3–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/Northampton_Town_F.C." title="Northampton Town F.C.">Northampton Town</a> in the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> third round; and in a 4–1 league win over <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> on 24 September.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> The following month he came runner-up to Portugal's <a href="/wiki/Renato_Sanches" title="Renato Sanches">Renato Sanches</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Boy_(award)" title="Golden Boy (award)">Golden Boy</a> award for best European player under the age of 21, on 24 October.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> As a player however he failed to score until 7 January 2017 when he scored a four-minute brace in the FA Cup against <a href="/wiki/Jaap_Stam" title="Jaap Stam">Jaap Stam</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Reading_F.C." title="Reading F.C.">Reading</a>, which ended 4–0.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rashford won his third trophy on 26 February in the <a href="/wiki/2017_EFL_Cup_Final" title="2017 EFL Cup Final">EFL Cup Final</a>, coming on as a 77th-minute substitute in the 3–2 victory over <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2017EFLC_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017EFLC-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> He was an instrumental part of United's 2–0 win over league leaders' <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> on 16 April, scoring the first goal after seven minutes from <a href="/wiki/Ander_Herrera" title="Ander Herrera">Ander Herrera</a>'s through ball.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Rashford scored another key goal four days later against <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a> in the 107th minute of the Europa League quarter-final second leg in a 2–1 win (3–2 on aggregate), sending United into the next round.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> He started in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Europa League Final">Europa League Final</a> on 24 May against Dutch team <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>, which Manchester United won 2–0 thus earning his fourth, and first European, trophy.<sup id="cite_ref-2017UEL_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017UEL-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Due to the signing of Ibrahimovi, Rashford spent the majority of the season on the wing. He made the most appearances of any United player during the season, playing 53 times.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg/170px-Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="344" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg/255px-Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e7/Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="297" data-file-height="601" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Marcus_Rashford_2017-11-05_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rashford in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Rashford made his first appearance of his <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Manchester United F.C. season">second full senior season</a> on 8 August 2017 against Real Madrid in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2017 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a> as a 46th-minute substitute in a 2–1 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> He started in a 4–0 home win against West Ham United five days later on 13 August, providing the assist for <a href="/wiki/Romelu_Lukaku" title="Romelu Lukaku">Romelu Lukaku</a>'s opening goal.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Rashford scored his first goal of the season on 26 August, the opener in a 2–0 victory over Leicester, three minutes after coming on as a substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> On 12 September, Rashford scored against <a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">Basel</a> on his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut, the third in a 3–0 win, marking the sixth competition that he has scored in on his debut.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> He scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Burton_Albion_F.C." title="Burton Albion F.C.">Burton Albion</a> on 20 September in EFL Cup third round, as well as assisting the fourth goal in a 4–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 23 October, Rashford came third in the 2017 Golden Boy award behind winner <a href="/wiki/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9" title="Kylian Mbappé">Kylian Mbappé</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ousmane_Demb%C3%A9l%C3%A9" title="Ousmane Dembélé">Ousmane Dembélé</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> By 28 October, Rashford had contributed to 12 goals in 16 games, with seven goals and five assists, with his most recent goal being against <a href="/wiki/Huddersfield_Town_A.F.C." title="Huddersfield Town A.F.C.">Huddersfield Town</a> on 21 October and his most recent assist coming against <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a> on 24 October.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On 6 December, he put in a man of the match performance in a 2–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/PFC_CSKA_Moscow" title="PFC CSKA Moscow">CSKA Moscow</a>, scoring the winning goal to help United qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">knockout phase</a> of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> In the January transfer window, the club signed <a href="/wiki/Alexis_S%C3%A1nchez" title="Alexis Sánchez">Alexis Sánchez</a>, threatening Rashford's future in the team.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 10 March 2018, Rashford scored both goals in a 2–1 win over rivals <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> on his first Premier League start of the year.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, United were eliminated from the Champions League after a 2–1 defeat to Spanish side <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a>, with Rashford producing the assist for United's goal.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Mourinho was criticised for playing Rashford out of position on the right wing, where he was unable to play with any "spontaneity and freedom".<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> Rashford scored in United's last game of the season on 13 May, a 1–0 victory over Watford at Old Trafford.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> At the conclusion of the season, Mourinho rejected the possibility of Rashford leaving on loan, pointing out Rashford had been selected for almost every match of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Definitely he can be absolutely top-class. He is only 21 but the maturity he is showing at times is more than 21 and his work rate".</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—United manager <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskjær">Ole Gunnar Solskjær</a> compared Rashford to <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wayne_Rooney" title="Wayne Rooney">Wayne Rooney</a> when he made his 150th appearance during the season.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Prior to the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2018–19 Manchester United F.C. season">2018–19 season</a>, Rashford was given the squad number 10 following the release of Ibrahimovi, the club's previous number 10.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> The shirt had also previously been worn in the Premier League by <a href="/wiki/Teddy_Sheringham" title="Teddy Sheringham">Teddy Sheringham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ruud_van_Nistelrooy" title="Ruud van Nistelrooy">Ruud van Nistelrooy</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wayne_Rooney" title="Wayne Rooney">Wayne Rooney</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> and he was the third academy graduate to wear it after <a href="/wiki/Mark_Hughes" title="Mark Hughes">Mark Hughes</a> and <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David Beckham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> On 2 September, Rashford was sent off in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a> at <a href="/wiki/Turf_Moor" title="Turf Moor">Turf Moor</a> after clashing heads with <a href="/wiki/Phil_Bardsley" title="Phil Bardsley">Phil Bardsley</a>, having only been on the pitch for 10 minutes;<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> Mourinho labelled him "naïve", and put it down to inexperience.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> On 11 September, <i><a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports" title="Sky Sports">Sky Sports</a></i> pundit <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Carragher" title="Jamie Carragher">Jamie Carragher</a> opined that Rashford would have to leave United to reach his potential, having not started a game in the season at that point.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Mourinho defended his use of Rashford in the team, suggesting that other clubs did not give youth players the same game time Rashford had recorded in the prior two seasons;<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> he started his first game and subsequently scored his first goal of the season on 29 September in a 3–1 loss to West Ham United.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> On 3 November, he scored again, providing a winning goal in the second minute of stoppage time in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/AFC_Bournemouth" title="AFC Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 December, Rashford provided both assists in United's 2–2 draw with Southampton, with the goals coming from Lukaku and Herrera.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> The following Saturday against <a href="/wiki/Fulham_F.C." title="Fulham F.C.">Fulham</a>, he provided two assists for <a href="/wiki/Ashley_Young" title="Ashley Young">Ashley Young</a> and Juan Mata before scoring the final goal in a 4–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> On 12 December, Rashford came on as substitute for midfielder <a href="/wiki/Fred_(footballer,_born_1993)" title="Fred (footballer, born 1993)">Fred</a> and scored a header in the 87th minute in a 2–1 loss to Spanish team <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> in the final <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_H" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> match of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> On 22 December, Rashford scored in the third minute of Manchester United's first match under new interim manager <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskjær">Ole Gunnar Solskjær</a>, in which United beat <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_City_F.C." title="Cardiff City F.C.">Cardiff City</a> 5–1.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> On 30 December, Rashford again scored against Bournemouth in his final game of 2018, also assisting <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a>'s first goal in United's 4–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> Solskjær praised Rashford's performances during the beginning of his reign, describing him as "different class", and said he thought Rashford had the chance to become one of the best strikers in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> During United's first match of 2019 on 2 January, Rashford assisted the <i>Red Devils<span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span></i> first goal from a free kick and scored the second in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> at <a href="/wiki/St_James%27_Park" title="St James&#39; Park">St James' Park</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Following this series of performances, pundit <a href="/wiki/Gary_Neville" title="Gary Neville">Gary Neville</a> praised Rashford for beginning to play beyond just his potential, establishing himself as a "devastating" forward player.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 January, Rashford scored the only goal in a 1–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> this marked the first time he had scored in three successive league games in his career,<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> the third youngest to achieve this for United behind only Rooney and Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> The following week, he made his 150th appearance for the club in a 2–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion_F.C." title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion F.C.">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> scoring a solo goal to become the youngest player in United's history to score in four successive league games,<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> and the fourth youngest to reach 150 games, behind <a href="/wiki/Norman_Whiteside" title="Norman Whiteside">Norman Whiteside</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Best" title="George Best">George Best</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Giggs" title="Ryan Giggs">Ryan Giggs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> On 2 February, Rashford was announced as Manchester United's Player of the Month for January 2019,<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> as well as winning United's goal of the month for his strike against Tottenham.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> A day later, he made his 100th league appearance for the club and scored the only goal in a 1–0 away victory over Leicester City. In doing so, he became the second-youngest player after Giggs to reach the milestone for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> His impressive performance in January earned him his first <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> title,<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> becoming the first United player since Ibrahimovi in December 2016 to win the award.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 March, Rashford scored from his first competitive penalty for the club, sealing a 3–1 win in the second leg of their <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Round_of_16" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League round of 16 tie</a> against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> to send the club through to the quarter-final on the <a href="/wiki/Away_goals_rule" title="Away goals rule">away goals rule</a>; he also contributed to Lukaku's equaliser, who scored off the rebound from Rashford's initial shot.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Solskjær described him as "fearless" for taking the penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> On 30 March, Rashford scored the opening goal in United's first victory with Solskjær as permanent manager, beating Watford 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season:_COVID-19_.26_Project_Restart"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season:_COVID-19_&amp;_Project_Restart">2019–20 season: COVID-19 &amp; Project Restart</span></h3>
<p>On 1 July 2019, Rashford signed a new four-year contract with Manchester United, keeping him at the club until June 2023, with the option to extend by a further year.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> On the opening week of the season, Rashford scored a brace in a 4–0 win over Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> In September 2019, following a spell of poor form, Solskjær said he was not concerned about Rashford's dip in form and lack of goals.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Towards the end of October, a return to form saw Rashford score in a 1–1 <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C.%E2%80%93Manchester_United_F.C._rivalry" title="Liverpool F.C.–Manchester United F.C. rivalry">North West derby</a> draw, ending rival's Liverpool's 17 match winning streak.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> The following week, Rashford scored and assisted against <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> and scored a second brace against Chelsea in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_EFL_Cup" title="2019–20 EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> The return to form sparked by the Liverpool goal saw Rashford go on the best goalscoring run of his career to date, scoring 16 club goals in 20 matches,<sup id="cite_ref-sb1920_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sb1920-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> ending the run with a brace in a 4–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> Rashford suffered a double <a href="/wiki/Stress_fracture" title="Stress fracture">stress fracture</a> to the back in the following game, an FA Cup tie against <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a>, which put him out of action for several months.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> By playing in the game, he became the fourth youngest United player to have played 200 games for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-BT200_122-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BT200-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The season was halted for over three months, following a decision on 13 March 2020 by the Premier League to suspend the league after a number of players and other club staff became ill due to the COVID-19 pandemic. In May 2020, manager Solskjær announced that Rashford would be fit to play following the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League#Effects_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic" title="2019–20 Premier League">return to football during project restart</a>, which saw the Premier League season resume behind closed doors for the remainder of the season. <sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> On 4 July, he scored his first goal since the restart as United beat Bournemouth 5–2.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> On 16 July, he scored his 17th Premier League goal of the season in a 2–0 victory against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>, equalling his tally in the two previous seasons combined.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> At the end of season, Rashford was voted third for the English <a href="/wiki/FWA_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="FWA Footballer of the Year">FWA Footballer of the Year</a> award,<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> he also received the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Merit_Award" title="PFA Merit Award">PFA Merit Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Marcus is talented enough and grounded enough and driven enough to be a legend at this club. In and around the dressing room as well, he is a Man United boy through and through. I am absolutely delighted with his contribution and he knows what Man United is all about. He has the DNA".</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> manager <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskjær">Ole Gunnar Solskjær</a>, praising Rashford's potential in December 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 26 September 2020, Rashford scored his first goal of the season in a 3–2 win against Brighton &amp; Hove Albion.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> On 20 October 2020, he scored the winning goal in a 2–1 away win against PSG in the first match of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">2020–21 Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> In the next Champions League match, Rashford scored his first United hat-trick in a 5–0 win over <a href="/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> it was the second hat-trick ever scored by a United substitute, following manager Solskjær in the <a href="/wiki/Nottingham_Forest_F.C._1%E2%80%938_Manchester_United_F.C." title="Nottingham Forest F.C. 1–8 Manchester United F.C.">Premier League in 1999</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> He became the sixth United player to score a <a href="/wiki/List_of_UEFA_Champions_League_hat-tricks" title="List of UEFA Champions League hat-tricks">Champions League hat-trick</a>, and the first since <a href="/wiki/Robin_van_Persie" title="Robin van Persie">Robin van Persie</a> <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Manchester_United_v_Olympiacos" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">in 2014</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Rashford suffered a shoulder injury during a 3–1 victory against Everton;<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> he continued to play despite the injury, but completed only one full game over the following month.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> On 26 December, Rashford became the third youngest Manchester United player to score 50 Premier League goals, when he scored the opening goal in the away fixture against <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> that ended in a 2–2 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 January 2021, Rashford assisted a goal for Pogba to score the only goal of the game against Burnley, which resulted in United being top of the table or the first time since the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2012–13 Manchester United F.C. season">2012–13 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> On 2 February, he scored the second goal in United's Premier League record-equalling <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C._9%E2%80%930_Southampton_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C. 9–0 Southampton F.C.">9–0</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> During a 1–0 win against West Ham in the FA Cup on 9 February, Rashford made his 250th appearance for the club, becoming the fourth youngest to reach the milestone.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span></h3>
<p>In 2012, Rashford was invited to an <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-16_football_team" title="England national under-16 football team">England under-16</a> training camp,<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> and was later selected to play in the <a href="/wiki/Victory_Shield" title="Victory Shield">Victory Shield</a> against <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland_national_under-16_football_team" title="Northern Ireland national under-16 football team">Northern Ireland under-16s</a> in September,<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_under-16_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Wales national under-16 football team">Wales under-16s</a> in October.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> Under-16's manager <a href="/wiki/Kenny_Swain" title="Kenny Swain">Kenny Swain</a> later revealed that Rashford only played two appearances for the side due to an understanding with coaches at Manchester United regarding him being underdeveloped physically, and also thought the exposure would have been "too much" for him.<sup id="cite_ref-RashRise_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashRise-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Three weeks after making his senior début for United in early 2016, Rashford made his first appearance for the <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-20_football_team" title="England national under-20 football team">England under-20 team</a>, providing an assist for <a href="/wiki/Kasey_Palmer" title="Kasey Palmer">Kasey Palmer</a> in a 2–1 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Canada_men%27s_national_under-20_soccer_team" title="Canada men&#39;s national under-20 soccer team">Canada under-20s</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> Despite already making his senior début earlier in the year, Rashford was called up to the <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-21_football_team" title="England national under-21 football team">England under-21 team</a> for the first time in August 2016 for a fixture in September against <a href="/wiki/Norway_national_under-21_football_team" title="Norway national under-21 football team">Norway under-21s</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> He scored a hat-trick in a 6–1 in his only appearance for the team,<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> scoring the third with a penalty, his first since turning professional.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> Under-21 manager <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Southgate" title="Gareth Southgate">Gareth Southgate</a> praised Rashford for his humility in dropping down to under-21 level.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite having already made his senior tournament début, it was expected Rashford would be available for selection for the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2017 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2017 UEFA European Under-21 Championship</a>, with the hopes of gaining more tournament experience.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> United manager José Mourinho responded to these reports by stating it would make no sense for his development as he was already playing senior football.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> In April 2017, Mourinho appeared to concede Rashford would attend the tournament, saying he had no right to stop him from participating,<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> but later in the month reiterated his opinion that dropping down wouldn't make sense, with Rashford having gained so much senior experience throughout the season.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> In May, Rashford made the decision not to go to the tournament,<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> and was instead selected for the senior squad by Southgate, the new manager.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> Southgate praised the decisions taken by United coaching staff in helping maximise the potential of Rashford by not allowing him exposure at youth level for England, saying his development had been handled well by all parties.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.932018:_first_major_tournaments"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–2018:_first_major_tournaments">2016–2018: first major tournaments</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:A54i7100.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/A54i7100.jpg/220px-A54i7100.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/A54i7100.jpg/330px-A54i7100.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/A54i7100.jpg/440px-A54i7100.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:A54i7100.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rashford playing for <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>Rashford's performances in his first senior season led to calls for him to represent <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>. Manchester United academy coach <a href="/wiki/Nicky_Butt" title="Nicky Butt">Nicky Butt</a> dismissed these calls, calling them premature and possibly harmful for the player's development,<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> as did England manager <a href="/wiki/Roy_Hodgson" title="Roy Hodgson">Roy Hodgson</a>, who said Rashford should be allowed to "develop in peace".<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> In April, Hodgson admitted it was "unlikely" Rashford would be included in his tournament squad,<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> but on 16 May, Hodgson named him in his preliminary 26-man squad for the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> He became part of England's Euro 2016 squad less than four months after making his United debut.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 May, he started in a warm-up match against <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_soccer_team" title="Australia national soccer team">Australia</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stadium_of_Light" title="Stadium of Light">Stadium of Light</a> and scored the opening goal of a 2–1 win after three minutes, becoming the youngest Englishman to score on his international debut,<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> and the third youngest overall. The previous youngest scoring debutant was <a href="/wiki/Tommy_Lawton" title="Tommy Lawton">Tommy Lawton</a> in 1938.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> On 16 June, he replaced <a href="/wiki/Adam_Lallana" title="Adam Lallana">Adam Lallana</a> in the 73rd minute of England's 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_football_team" title="Wales national football team">Wales</a> at Euro 2016, making his tournament debut at the age of 18 years and 229 days, becoming England's youngest ever player at a European Championships and breaking <a href="/wiki/Wayne_Rooney" title="Wayne Rooney">Wayne Rooney</a>'s <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004" title="UEFA Euro 2004">Euro 2004</a> record by four days.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> He played just one more game in the tournament, coming on as a late substitute in England's shock 2–1 loss to <a href="/wiki/Iceland_national_football_team" title="Iceland national football team">Iceland</a> in which he was praised for his impact,<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> but described it as a valuable experience.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>New England manager <a href="/wiki/Sam_Allardyce" title="Sam Allardyce">Sam Allardyce</a> told Rashford he would not be called up to his first squad for a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Slovakia_national_football_team" title="Slovakia national football team">Slovakia</a> in September, citing his lack of playing time in the early stages of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> Allardyce was quickly replaced by Southgate, and Rashford was recalled to the senior team for games against <a href="/wiki/Malta_national_football_team" title="Malta national football team">Malta</a> and <a href="/wiki/Slovenia_national_football_team" title="Slovenia national football team">Slovenia</a> in October.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> Rashford scored his first competitive goal for the senior team on 4 September 2017, with the winning goal in England's 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Slovakia_national_football_team" title="Slovakia national football team">Slovakia</a> in <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> He was named in the 23-man England squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> Rashford scored the opening goal of England's final warm-up match against <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica_national_football_team" title="Costa Rica national football team">Costa Rica</a> on 7 June 2018,<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> and was tipped by former England stars <a href="/wiki/Chris_Waddle" title="Chris Waddle">Chris Waddle</a> and <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Hoddle" title="Glenn Hoddle">Glenn Hoddle</a> to start England's opening match against <a href="/wiki/Tunisia_national_football_team" title="Tunisia national football team">Tunisia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> He started the game on the bench, but came on and performed well after replacing <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a>, deemed to be his direct competition for the starting role.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> He was reportedly set to start the second game against <a href="/wiki/Panama_national_football_team" title="Panama national football team">Panama</a> due to the potential physically posed by their opposition,<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> but Southgate ultimately changed his mind,<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> Having already qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage" title="2018 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">knockout stage</a>, he started England's final group game against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a> alongside <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Vardy" title="Jamie Vardy">Jamie Vardy</a>, but failed to impress.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> Rashford came on as a substitute and scored in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Colombia_vs_England" title="2018 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">Round of 16</a> penalty shoot-out against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> which saw England progress to the quarter-final,<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> ultimately finishing fourth overall – their best performance since 1990.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.93present"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–present">2018–present</span></h4>
<p>On 8 September 2018, Rashford scored at Wembley in England's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a> opener against <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>, losing 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Rashford also scored in a 1–0 friendly win over <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a> at the <a href="/wiki/King_Power_Stadium" title="King Power Stadium">King Power Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup> The following month, he scored a goal and provided an assist in a 3–2 away win against Spain.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> England's final Nations League game on 18 November saw Rashford play in a 2–1 win over Croatia that saw England top their group and qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Nations_League_Finals" title="2019 UEFA Nations League Finals">Nations League finals</a> in June 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> His appearance in this game saw Rashford equal a national record set by <a href="/wiki/Jack_Charlton" title="Jack Charlton">Jack Charlton</a> in 1966 by playing a total of 16 games for England throughout the year.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-final, Rashford scored the opening goal of the game against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>, however England lost 3–1 in extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the 2019 October internationals, Rashford scored his first goal in England's qualification campaign for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying">Euro 2020</a> in a 6–0 away victory over <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria_national_football_team" title="Bulgaria national football team">Bulgaria</a> on 14 October.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> Rashford also scored in both of England's November international, a 7–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Montenegro_national_football_team" title="Montenegro national football team">Montenegro</a> and a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Kosovo_national_football_team" title="Kosovo national football team">Kosovo</a>. These wins saw England become the ninth team to qualify for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020" title="UEFA Euro 2020">Euro 2020</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id="Style_of_play.2C_development_and_comparisons"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play,_development_and_comparisons">Style of play, development and comparisons</span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"When you are on the left, you can create a lot more things on your own, giving that little bit more to the team. Whereas when you are playing up front, sometimes you are isolated and need someone in midfield who can find passes for 90 minutes of a game, so you can disappear in games sometimes as a No.9. When I transitioned to a No.9 when I was younger, that's the bit that I struggled with as I was always someone who wanted to express myself on the ball. When I started playing No.9, I realised that you don't see the ball as often as you do in other positions, but when you do see the ball, it's an opportunity to score goals. That's what I loved about being a No.9 and that's what I still love about it. But right now I’m enjoying having the freedom to mix between the two".</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Rashford discussing his best position.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Rashford can play as either a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre forward</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a>, primarily on the left-wing.<sup id="cite_ref-RashCV_188-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashCV-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Optus_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Optus-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> Rashford himself prefers playing on the left, a position which allows him to cut inside and strike on goal with his stronger right foot, and likes to drop deep to collect the ball and build an attack, something he learned as a youngster when playing as a central midfielder following a battle with <a href="/wiki/Osgood%E2%80%93Schlatter_disease" title="Osgood–Schlatter disease">Osgood–Schlatter disease</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Optus_190-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Optus-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> In his formative years, Rashford's former youth coach <a href="/wiki/Paul_McGuinness_(footballer)" title="Paul McGuinness (footballer)">Paul McGuinness</a> noted how he was attempting to play similarly to Italian midfielder <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Pirlo" title="Andrea Pirlo">Andrea Pirlo</a>, but he and fellow coaches <a href="/wiki/Warren_Joyce" title="Warren Joyce">Warren Joyce</a> and <a href="/wiki/Colin_Little" title="Colin Little">Colin Little</a> saw Rashford's potential at a striker and helped him work on his body shape and various attacking runs.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> They advised him to focus on being a goalscorer rather than a creative player, and to use his pace to make runs behind the defence.<sup id="cite_ref-Rash12_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rash12-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> His coaches were reminded of <a href="/wiki/Danny_Welbeck" title="Danny Welbeck">Danny Welbeck</a> due to his versatility, but it was decided to instead teach him the "art" of goalscoring, instructing him how to make runs at the right time, and was held back from playing reserve team football to give him confidence in his goalscoring abilities by pitting him against lesser defences.<sup id="cite_ref-FFTMWMH_19-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FFTMWMH-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Rashford says his versatility can enable him to become the "ultimate centre forward".<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rashford is a pacey and direct player,<sup id="cite_ref-RashCV_188-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashCV-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Optus_190-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Optus-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Rash365_194-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rash365-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> and often moves to central positions to create chances and get into goalscoring positions.<sup id="cite_ref-BT200_122-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BT200-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup> He constantly tests defenders both with his movement and positioning off the ball, meaning opponents often double up on him.<sup id="cite_ref-RashCV_188-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RashCV-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> Rashford's former United manager <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> has said he is "not a target man, he is a man of movement. I do not think he is a pure nine",<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> comments echoed by his manager with England, <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Southgate" title="Gareth Southgate">Gareth Southgate</a>, who has said his ability to play with his back to goal and his hold-up play weren't his major strengths, and is better suited as a "wide raider" coming in off the wing.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> His current manager at United, <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskjær">Ole Gunnar Solskjær</a>, has been credited with improving him as a player and helping him mature by giving him freedom as a winger he hadn't previously experienced.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> Rashford's main attributes also include his <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> ability,<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> and his "ruthless" finishing ability, which has been compared to that of former United striker <a href="/wiki/Ruud_van_Nistelrooy" title="Ruud van Nistelrooy">Ruud van Nistelrooy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> a player McGuinness advised him to study while they worked together in the club's academy.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> Rashford understands the need for a striker to be able to score different kinds of goals to be a player who can score 20-25 per season,<sup id="cite_ref-BT200_122-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BT200-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> and is said to be a player with composure and awareness.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> Rashford often takes <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalties</a> and <a href="/wiki/Free_kick_(association_football)" title="Free kick (association football)">free kicks</a> for United,<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> and has been known to use the <i><a href="/wiki/Knuckleball#Association_football" title="Knuckleball">knuckleball</a></i> technique on set pieces, which was popularised by former United player <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His success has been credited to his drive and personal ambition both on and off the pitch, and is viewed as a role model for younger players like <a href="/wiki/Mason_Greenwood" title="Mason Greenwood">Mason Greenwood</a> due to his success at a young age.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup> He attributes his "focus and dedication" to watching and listening to former United striker <a href="/wiki/Robin_van_Persie" title="Robin van Persie">Robin van Persie</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup> and recalls seeing pictures of former academy players such as <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David Beckham</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paul_Scholes" title="Paul Scholes">Paul Scholes</a> on the walls of <a href="/wiki/Trafford_Training_Centre" title="Trafford Training Centre">Carrington</a>, United's training centre, and being determined to reach the same level they had.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNJourney_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNJourney-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> According to McGuinness he was always professional and mature,<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> and even at a young age, has been described as a leader,<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> with former United and England midfielder <a href="/wiki/Owen_Hargreaves" title="Owen Hargreaves">Owen Hargreaves</a> saying he has the characteristics to be a <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> Rashford has praised former teammate <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> and Mourinho with helping improve his mentality, describing their combined influence as key to his development.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> He has been described as a "big game player" due to his performances and contributions in important matches,<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> including on several débuts for club and country.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> Rashford has also received
